<td style="vertical-align:top;padding-top:15px;width:50%">
<div>&nbsp;</div>
<div style="background-color: #FFFFFF;padding:10px; clear: both;">
<a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Welcome,_newcomers" title="Wiktionary:Welcome, newcomers">Welcome</a> to the English-language Wiktionary, a collaborative project to produce a free-content multilingual dictionary. It aims to describe all words of all languages using definitions and descriptions in English.</div>
<div style="background-color: #FFFFFF;padding:10px;">
Wiktionary has grown beyond a standard dictionary and now includes a <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Thesaurus" title="Wiktionary:Thesaurus">thesaurus</a>, a rhyme guide, phrase books, language statistics and extensive appendices.  We aim to include not only the definition of a word, but also enough information to really understand it. Thus <a href="/wiki/etymology" title="etymology">etymologies</a>, pronunciations, sample quotations, synonyms, antonyms and translations are included.</div>
<div style="background-color: #FFFFFF;padding:10px;">
Wiktionary is a <a href="/wiki/wiki" title="wiki">wiki</a>, which means that you can edit it, and all the content is dual-licensed under both the <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Text_of_Creative_Commons_Attribution-ShareAlike_3.0_Unported_License" title="Wiktionary:Text of Creative Commons Attribution-ShareAlike 3.0 Unported License">Creative Commons Attribution-ShareAlike 3.0 Unported License</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:GNU_Free_Documentation_License" title="Wiktionary:GNU Free Documentation License">GNU Free Documentation License</a>. Before you contribute, you may wish to read through some of <a href="/wiki/Help:Contents" title="Help:Contents">our help pages</a>, and bear in mind that we do things quite differently from other wikis. In particular, we have strict <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Entry_layout" title="Wiktionary:Entry layout">layout conventions</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Criteria_for_inclusion" title="Wiktionary:Criteria for inclusion">inclusion criteria</a>. Learn how to <a href="/wiki/Help:Starting_a_new_page" title="Help:Starting a new page">start a page</a>, how to <a href="/wiki/Help:How_to_edit_a_page" title="Help:How to edit a page">edit entries</a>, experiment in the <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Sandbox" title="Wiktionary:Sandbox">sandbox</a> and visit our <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Community_Portal" title="Wiktionary:Community Portal">Community Portal</a> to see how you can participate in the development of Wiktionary.</div>
</td>

<td colspan="2"><div style="float:right;" class="plainlinks"><small class="editlink"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Word_of_the_day/2022/April_19&amp;action=edit">edit</a></small><small class="editlink">&nbsp;· <a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Main_Page&amp;action=purge">refresh</a>&nbsp;· <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Word_of_the_day/2022/April_19" title="Wiktionary:Word of the day/2022/April 19">view</a></small></div><div style="font-size:150%; border-bottom:1px solid #AAAAAA; padding-left:40px; line-height:22px">Word of the day<span style="font-size:small;"><br>for <span id="WOTD-rss-date">April 19</span></span></div>

<tr>
<td><b><a href="/wiki/calcine#English" title="calcine"><span id="WOTD-rss-title">calcine</span></a></b> <i>v</i>
</td></tr>

<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="float:right"><span class="mw-tmh-player audio" style="width:220px;"><audio id="mwe_player_0_placeholder" preload="none" width="220" style="width:220px;" data-durationhint="2" data-mwtitle="LL-Q1860_(eng)-Vealhurl-calcine.wav" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" disabled="disabled" tabindex="-1"></audio><a class="mw-tmh-play" href="/wiki/File:LL-Q1860_(eng)-Vealhurl-calcine.wav" title="Play media" role="button"><span class="mw-tmh-play-icon"></span></a><span class="mw-tmh-duration mw-tmh-label" aria-label="2 seconds">0:02</span></span></div><div id="WOTD-rss-description">
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/alchemy" title="alchemy">alchemy</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#historical" title="Appendix:Glossary">historical</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/heat#Verb" title="heat">heat</a> (a <a href="/wiki/substance#Noun" title="substance">substance</a>) to <a href="/wiki/remove#Verb" title="remove">remove</a> its <a href="/wiki/impurity" title="impurity">impurities</a> and <a href="/wiki/refine" title="refine">refine</a> it.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/chemistry" title="chemistry">chemistry</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To heat (a substance) without <a href="/wiki/melting#Noun" title="melting">melting</a> in order to <a href="/wiki/drive_off" title="drive off">drive off</a> <a href="/wiki/water#Noun" title="water">water</a>, etc., and to <a href="/wiki/oxidize" title="oxidize">oxidize</a> or <a href="/wiki/reduce" title="reduce">reduce</a> it; specifically, to <a href="/wiki/decompose" title="decompose">decompose</a> (<a href="/wiki/carbonate" title="carbonate">carbonates</a>) into <a href="/wiki/oxide" title="oxide">oxides</a>, and, especially, to heat (<a href="/wiki/limestone" title="limestone">limestone</a>) to <a href="/wiki/form#Verb" title="form">form</a> <a href="/wiki/quicklime" title="quicklime">quicklime</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To heat (something) to <a href="/wiki/dry#Verb" title="dry">dry</a> and <a href="/wiki/sterilize" title="sterilize">sterilize</a> it.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figuratively</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<ol><li>To <a href="/wiki/purify" title="purify">purify</a> or refine (something).</li>
<li>To <a href="/wiki/burn_up#Verb" title="burn up">burn up</a> (something) <a href="/wiki/completely" title="completely">completely</a>; to <a href="/wiki/incinerate" title="incinerate">incinerate</a>; hence, to <a href="/wiki/destroy" title="destroy">destroy</a> (something).</li></ol></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/chemistry" title="chemistry">chemistry</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of a substance: to <a href="/wiki/undergo" title="undergo">undergo</a> <a href="/wiki/heating#Noun" title="heating">heating</a> so as to <a href="/wiki/oxidize" title="oxidize">oxidize</a> it.</li></ol>
<p><b><a href="/wiki/calcine#Noun" title="calcine">calcine</a></b> <i>n</i>
</p>
<ol><li>Something <a href="/wiki/calcine#Verb" title="calcine">calcined</a>; also, <a href="/wiki/material#Noun" title="material">material</a> <a href="/wiki/leave#Verb" title="leave">left</a> over after <a href="/wiki/burning#Noun" title="burning">burning</a> or <a href="/wiki/roasting#Noun" title="roasting">roasting</a>.</li></ol>
</div>
</td></tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wiktionaries_in_other_languages" data-mw-comment="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;heading&quot;,&quot;level&quot;:0,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;h-Wiktionaries_in_other_languages&quot;,&quot;replies&quot;:[],&quot;headingLevel&quot;:3,&quot;placeholderHeading&quot;:false,&quot;name&quot;:&quot;h-&quot;}"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Wiktionaries_in_other_languages"></span>Wiktionaries in other languages<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Wiktionaries_in_other_languages"></span></span></h3>
<p>This is the <a href="/wiki/English" title="English">English</a>-language Wiktionary, where words from all languages are defined in English. For example, see the entry for the French word <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/dictionnaire#French" title="dictionnaire">dictionnaire</a></i>. To find a French definition of that word, visit the equivalent page <a href="https://fr.wiktionary.org/wiki/dictionnaire" class="extiw" title="fr:dictionnaire">in the French Wiktionary</a>. <br><br>
